Located in a strip mall this place leaves a lot to be desired for the prices they charge.

CONS: Service was slow and server forgetful.
Had to ask for a fork and drinks twice. One she took orders only came back once to ask if anything else was needed and there was only 2 other couples there eating.
To get to the restrooms you have to walk thru a service area where food is located and the men's room opens directly into that area!!!
The restrooms are disgusting. Caked in grime along edges and corners of restroom floor.
Food was just ok.. probably better at Panda Express or anywhere else.

PROS
The chef was great and friendly</text>

I am absolutely blown away that this place has 4 stars.. I live right down the street and decided to stop and get some sushi to-go. $35.00 and 25 minutes later, I finally leave with 5 different rolls. Get to the house and immediately notice a funny smell coming from the boxes. I proceed against my better judgment and immediately spit it out. EACH AND EVERY ROLL TASTE LIKE PLASTIC. Both I and my buddy tried each roll and couldn't stomach the taste enough to even swallow the roll... Half the fish was discolored or obviously dyed, The rice was undercooked.  There was a plastic smell and taste, in each and every roll. (It is hard to describe, but trust me, it was not edible) All in All. Huge waste of $35.00 and time. Will never recommend or step foot in this location again.  I recommend everyone does the same unless you want food poisoning...</Text>

The best and my most favorite Japanese teppan bar in town.  Good prices and great food.  I have been going there for 30 years and even though they have had a change of ownership over the years, the food has NEVER been less than perfect.  I always get the Hibachi Steak and Shrimp. I'm so very hungry now...<//review>

<user_id>103267608606459576297< /user_id><user_name>Charles Fukushima< /user_name><Date>1531977318503< /Date><Rate>3< /Rate><Review>Very humble location which was clean and had friendly and helpful staff. The selection and pricing of what is offered (sushi and traditional Japanese eatery) was definitely fair for what they offered in terms of quantity, but was definitely lacking in quality.

Overall anything cooked from this place is good; however, with lack of good central air or great refrigeration for their fish, I would err on the side of caution when getting their raw sushi, especially on a hot day.

Entering the restaurant, the temperature inside was definitely a problem as it was hardly different from the outside (~100 ¬∞F).

As it was so hot outside and in, the effect of the heat was completely noticeable on the sushi. Overall the cut rolls offered were fine as any major fish flaw was covered up by their pairing and combination of sauces and seasoning; however, all nigiri served was questionable in edibility and quality. From first taste you can completely tell that the fish is "dead." It lacked flavour and freshness and felt almost as if the fish was old and stale. The nigiri also fell short at the fact that the fish itself felt luke warm and not chilled (as if the fish was left in the outside sun).</Review>< pics>

< Review>
I have to say, I'm pretty impressed! I have lived in Buena Park my entire life and have driven by this bowling alley soooo many times. I never went until Thursday night with some friends.
It's a really old bowling alley. My grandparents bowled here in their younger years so you can't expect it to be fancy at all.
The rates of their prices are awesome! It's per person, per game and the price fluctuates depending on the time you go. The great part about paying per game though is that you can take your time. The place I usually go to is by the hour so you have to bowl fast. I have my own shoes bit I think my friend said the shoe rental was $5.

The bar is open and you can order food. However everything is fried so if that's not your thing, eat before lol. I'll be back !!!<//Review>

< text>
Been on a bowling league there for over 11 years. They have remodeled and painted inside an out. It's to bad that they haven't put more money into fixing there bowling machine's. Always lanes breaking down, or your ball gets stuck back there, an it comes back with a nick or scratch, some times the pin setting is off to, (missing a few pins, on your first throw.) Now that they blocked off customers from eating in cafeteria, we have to wait longer for service girls to come down to take our orders. Poor girls are running ramped. (Need more, servers during big bowling leagues playing). Oh an a BIG THING never fixed entire 11 + years I've been there, they have never fixed the girls bathroom sinks. One side only drips water, other one is a little better, but not by much, which ever side your on, the soap is empty or broken, so you have to run to other side to get soap or hand towels. So yea your walking with your bowling shoes on, now bottoms are wet from drips on bathroom floor. You gotta be careful bowling after that, you can slip and fall, or it stops you from gliding when you throw the ball.... Food prices are high $, but isn't any place, movies, bowling, park attractions. Etc.....
Other wise I love my bowling league family.<//text>
